     <p> The skeleton of a huge dragon is fossilised in one of the cliff faces here. Its wings are spread as if it was about to fly to the clouds one last time. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('8JeW9F0B');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Several caravans are circling a large camp fire on the edge of the cliffs, at the end of a winding steep trail.
